### [189] [EvoSchema: Towards Text-to-SQL Robustness Against Schema Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10697)
*Tianshu Zhang,Kun Qian,Siddhartha Sahai,Yuan Tian,Shaddy Garg,Huan Sun,Yunyao Li*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: EvoSchema是一个评估文本到SQL系统在数据库模式演化下鲁棒性的基准，包含10种扰动类型，发现表级扰动比列级扰动影响更大，训练数据增强能提升模型鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到SQL模型在静态模式上表现良好，但现实中的数据库模式会不断演化，导致模型性能下降。现有工作要么只关注简单的语法/语义映射，要么缺乏全面可控的方法来研究模式演化下的鲁棒性问题，这在面对日益复杂的数据模式变化时显得不足。

Method: 提出了EvoSchema基准，包含一个新颖的模式演化分类法，涵盖列级和表级修改的10种扰动类型，系统模拟数据库模式的动态变化。使用该基准对不同开源和闭源LLM进行深入评估。

Result: 评估发现表级扰动对模型性能的影响显著大于列级变化。在EvoSchema的多样化模式设计上训练的模型能够迫使模型区分相同问题的模式差异，避免学习虚假模式，相比在未扰动数据上训练的模型表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: EvoSchema为模型行为提供了有价值的见解，并为设计能够在动态现实环境中良好运行的系统指明了方向。该基准有助于开发更具弹性的文本到SQL系统，包括模型训练和数据库设计两方面。

Abstract: Neural text-to-SQL models, which translate natural language questions (NLQs) into SQL queries given a database schema, have achieved remarkable performance. However, database schemas frequently evolve to meet new requirements. Such schema evolution often leads to performance degradation for models trained on static schemas. Existing work either mainly focuses on simply paraphrasing some syntactic or semantic mappings among NLQ, DB and SQL, or lacks a comprehensive and controllable way to investigate the model robustness issue under the schema evolution, which is insufficient when facing the increasingly complex and rich database schema changes in reality, especially in the LLM era. To address the challenges posed by schema evolution, we present EvoSchema, a comprehensive benchmark designed to assess and enhance the robustness of text-to-SQL systems under real-world schema changes. EvoSchema introduces a novel schema evolution taxonomy, encompassing ten perturbation types across columnlevel and table-level modifications, systematically simulating the dynamic nature of database schemas. Through EvoSchema, we conduct an in-depth evaluation spanning different open source and closed-source LLMs, revealing that table-level perturbations have a significantly greater impact on model performance compared to column-level changes. Furthermore, EvoSchema inspires the development of more resilient text-to-SQL systems, in terms of both model training and database design. The models trained on EvoSchema's diverse schema designs can force the model to distinguish the schema difference for the same questions to avoid learning spurious patterns, which demonstrate remarkable robustness compared to those trained on unperturbed data on average. This benchmark offers valuable insights into model behavior and a path forward for designing systems capable of thriving in dynamic, real-world environments.

</details>


### [190] [Pneuma-Seeker: A Relational Reification Mechanism to Align AI Agents with Human Work over Relational Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10747)
*Muhammad Imam Luthfi Balaka,John Hillesland,Kemal Badur,Raul Castro Fernandez*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: Pneuma-Seeker是一个基于关系具体化的系统，通过将用户信息需求表示为关系模式，迭代优化并构建可执行程序来回答数据查询，相比现有方法具有更高准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据工作者常常无法精确表达信息需求，而LLM在处理意图不明确的查询时表现脆弱，容易产生幻觉、错误假设连接路径或给出无根据的答案。

Method: 采用关系具体化方法，将用户信息需求表示为关系模式，使用LLM驱动的智能体架构，通过指挥式规划和多级上下文管理，在异构关系语料库上迭代优化模式并构建可执行程序。

Result: 在多个领域评估中，Pneuma-Seeker相比最先进的学术和工业基线方法表现出更高的答案准确性。在实际组织部署中，验证了可信性和可检查性是LLM中介数据系统的关键需求。

Conclusion: Pneuma-Seeker通过关系具体化和智能体架构有效解决了LLM在数据查询中的脆弱性问题，为LLM中介的数据系统提供了可信和可检查的解决方案。

Abstract: When faced with data problems, many data workers cannot articulate their information need precisely enough for software to help. Although LLMs interpret natural-language requests, they behave brittly when intent is under-specified, e.g., hallucinating fields, assuming join paths, or producing ungrounded answers.
  We present Pneuma-Seeker, a system built around a central idea: relational reification. Pneuma-Seeker represents a user's evolving information need as a relational schema: a concrete, analysis-ready data model shared between user and system. Rather than answering prompts directly, Pneuma-Seeker iteratively refines this schema, then discovers and prepares relevant sources to construct a relation and executable program that compute the answer. Pneuma-Seeker employs an LLM-powered agentic architecture with conductor-style planning and macro- and micro-level context management to operate effectively over heterogeneous relational corpora.
  We evaluate Pneuma-Seeker across multiple domains against state-of-the-art academic and industrial baselines, demonstrating higher answer accuracy. Deployment in a real organization highlights trust and inspectability as essential requirements for LLM-mediated data systems.

</details>


### [191] [Beyond Standard Datacubes: Extracting Features from Irregular and Branching Earth System Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10809)
*Mathilde Leuridan,James Hawkes,Tiago Quintino,Martin Schultz*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出基于压缩树结构的广义数据超立方体表示法，用于高效处理地球科学中复杂、稀疏、不规则的数据空间，并集成特征提取系统实现精确数据访问。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球科学数据集在体积和结构复杂性上快速增长，传统密集正交的数据立方体模型难以高效表示不规则、稀疏或分支数据空间，需要新的数据表示方法。

Method: 1. 基于压缩树结构设计广义数据超立方体表示法；2. 在Polytope框架内构建集成特征提取系统；3. 将数据访问策略嵌入数据超立方体抽象中。

Result: 压缩树数据超立方体能够准确紧凑地描述复杂数据空间，捕获稀疏性和条件关系，作为大型后端数据存储的快速缓存式索引，支持精确的子字段数据提取。

Conclusion: 该工作弥合了表达性数据超立方体模型与高效数据访问方法之间的差距，为大规模异构地球科学数据集提供了可扩展、以用户为中心的访问基础。

Abstract: Earth science datasets are growing rapidly in both volume and structural complexity. They increasingly contain richly labelled data with heterogeneous metadata and complex internal constraints that impose dependencies between variables and dimensions. Datacubes have become a common abstraction for organising such datasets, but traditional dense and orthogonal datacube models struggle to represent irregular, sparse or branching data spaces efficiently. In this paper, we introduce a generalised data hypercube representation based on compressed tree structures, which enables an accurate and compact description of complex data spaces. We describe the design of this representation and analyse its ability to capture sparsity and conditional relationships while remaining efficient to traverse. Using a concrete implementation, we study the performance characteristics of compressed tree data hypercubes and demonstrate their effectiveness as fast, cache-like indices over large backend data stores. Building on this representation, we present an integrated feature extraction system that operates directly on tree-based data hypercubes within the Polytope framework. By embedding data access strategies into the data hypercube abstraction itself, the system enables precise, sub-field data extraction and supports flexible, user-driven access patterns. We evaluate the performance of the integrated system and show how it enables new ways of interacting with complex datasets that are difficult to support using traditional access models. This work bridges the gap between expressive data hypercube models and efficient data access methods. In particular, it provides a unified framework that combines tree-based data representations with feature extraction capabilities. The proposed approach therefore offers a foundation for scalable and user-centric access to large heterogeneous Earth science datasets.

</details>


### [192] [Poisson Sampling over Acyclic Joins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10982)
*Liese Bekkers,Frank Neven,Lorrens Pantelis,Stijn Vansummeren*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对无环连接的泊松采样算法，通过构建随机访问索引实现O(N + k log N)时间复杂度，显著优于重复伯努利试验方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在连接查询中实现高效的泊松采样（非均匀概率采样），避免完全物化连接结果，同时为查询引擎设计提供统一的处理基础。

Method: 构建随机访问索引，允许直接访问第i个连接元组而无需完全物化结果；使用该索引构建采样结果；在列存储中实现并优化工程权衡。

Result: 算法在真实数据上显著优于重复伯努利试验方法；随机访问索引本身也能高效实现Yannakakis无环连接算法，无需采样时同样具有竞争力。

Conclusion: 为查询引擎设计提供了统一基础，既能高效处理经典无环连接，又能实现泊松采样，相比传统方法均无性能损失。

Abstract: We introduce the problem of Poisson sampling over joins: compute a sample of the result of a join query by conceptually performing a Bernoulli trial for each join tuple, using a non-uniform and tuple-specific probability. We propose an algorithm for Poisson sampling over acyclic joins that is nearly instance-optimal, running in time O(N + k \log N) where N is the size of the input database, and k is the size of the resulting sample. Our algorithm hinges on two building blocks: (1) The construction of a random-access index that allows, given a number i, to randomly access the i-th join tuple without fully materializing the (possibly large) join result; (2) The probing of this index to construct the result sample. We study the engineering trade-offs required to make both components practical, focusing on their implementation in column stores, and identify best-performing alternatives for both. Our experiments on real-world data demonstrate that this pair of alternatives significantly outperforms the repeated-Bernoulli-trial algorithm for Poisson sampling while also demonstrating that the random-access index by itself can be used to competively implement Yannakakis' acyclic join processing algorithm when no sampling is required. This shows that, as far a query engine design is concerned, it is possible to adopt a uniform basis for both classical acyclic join processing and Poisson sampling, both without regret compared to classical join and sampling algorithms.

</details>
